  24 /* The following table can be generated from the file
  25     unix/mappings/eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt
  26    from the Unicode CD (also available on their FTP server) using
  27    the command
  28 
  29     egrep '^0x8[01234][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
  30       /mnt/cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt | perl ~/sjis.pl
  31 
  32    where sjis.pl contains:
  33 
  34   ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  35   while (<>) {
  36     local($sjis, $ucs, %rest) = split;
  37     $sjis = hex($sjis) - 0x8140;
  38     local($sidx) = int($sjis / 256) * 192 + ($sjis % 256);
  39     printf "\n " if (($n % 4) == 0);
  40     ++$n;
  41     printf " [%4d] = %s,", $sidx, $ucs;
  42   }
  43   print "\n";
  44   ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  45 */

1856 /* The following table can be generated using
1857 
1858    awk '/^0x/ { print $2, $1; }' < .../eastasia/jis/shiftjis.txt |
1859    egrep "^0x00[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]" |
1860    sort -u | perl tab.pl
1861 
1862    where tab.pl is
1863 
1864    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1865    $n=0;
1866    while (<>) {
1867      local($ucs4, $sjis, %rest) = split;
1868      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
1869      local($s)=hex($sjis);
1870      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 3 == 0);
1871      ++$n;
1872      printf (" [0x%04x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", $u,
1873          $s < 0x100 ? $s : int($s/256), $s < 0x100 ? 0 : $s&255);
1874    }
1875    printf ("\n");
1876    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1877 
1878    The only problem is that the shiftjis.txt file does not contain the
1879    mapping for the characters 0x00 to 0x1f.  We add them ourself.
1880 
1881    A much bigger problem is that mapping of the tilde and the backslash
1882    character.  There are no such characters in SJIS.  The proposed
1883    handling is to simply map the two input values to the corresponding
1884    byte values of ASCII.  Things fall more or less in place this way.
1885 */

4312 
4313 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
4314 #define CHARSET_NAME        "SJIS//"
4315 #define FROM_LOOP       from_sjis
4316 #define TO_LOOP         to_sjis
4317 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
4318 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
4319 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
4320 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     2
4321 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       4
4322 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0
4323 
4324 /* First define the conversion function from SJIS to UCS4.  */
4325 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4326 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4327 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
4328 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
4329 #define BODY \
4330   {                                       \
4331     uint32_t ch = *inptr;                             \
4332                                           \
4333     if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0x5c)                     \
4334       {                                       \
4335     ch = 0xa5;                                \
4336     ++inptr;                                  \
4337       }                                       \
4338     else if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0x7e)                    \
4339       {                                       \
4340     ch = 0x203e;                                  \
4341     ++inptr;                                  \
4342       }                                       \
4343     else if (ch < 0x80)                               \
4344       ++inptr;                                    \
4345     else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xdf)                        \
4346       {                                       \
4347     ch += 0xfec0;                                 \
4348     ++inptr;                                  \
4349       }                                       \
4350     else if (__builtin_expect (ch > 0xea, 0)                      \
4351          || __builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0xa0                  \
4352          || __builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0))                 \
4353       {                                       \
4354     /* These are illegal.  */                         \
4355     STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4356       }                                       \
4357     else                                      \
4358       {                                       \
4359     /* Two-byte character.  First test whether the next byte          \
4360        is also available.  */                         \
4361     uint32_t ch2;                                 \
4362     uint_fast32_t idx;                            \
4363                                           \
4364     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
4365       {                                   \
4366         /* The second byte is not available.  Store               \
4367            the intermediate result.  */                   \
4368         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
4369         break;                                \
4370       }                                   \
4371                                           \
4372     ch2 = inptr[1];                               \
4373     idx = ch * 256 + ch2;                             \
4374     if (__glibc_unlikely (ch2 < 0x40))                    \
4375       {                                   \
4376         /* This is illegal.  */                       \
4377         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4378       }                                   \
4379     else if ((__builtin_expect (idx > 0x84be && idx < 0x889f, 0))         \
4380          || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x88fc && idx < 0x8940, 0))      \
4381          || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x9ffc && idx < 0xe040, 0))      \
4382          || __builtin_expect (idx > 0xeaa4, 0))               \
4383       {                                   \
4384         /* This is illegal.  */                       \
4385         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2);                   \
4386       }                                   \
4387     else                                      \
4388       {                                   \
4389         /* We could pack the data a bit more dense.  The second       \
4390            byte will never be 0x7f and it will also be never          \
4391            >0xfc.  But this would mean yet more `if's.  */            \
4392         if (idx <= 0x84be)                            \
4393           ch = cjk_block1[(ch - 0x81) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4394         else if (idx <= 0x88fc)                       \
4395           ch = cjk_block2[(ch - 0x88) * 192 + ch2 - 0x9f];            \
4396         else if (idx <= 0x9ffc)                       \
4397           ch = cjk_block3[(ch - 0x89) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4398         else                                  \
4399           ch = cjk_block4[(ch - 0xe0) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4400                                           \
4401         if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == 0))                   \
4402           {                                   \
4403         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4404         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2);               \
4405           }                                   \
4406                                           \
4407         inptr += 2;                               \
4408       }                                   \
4409       }                                       \
4410                                           \
4411     put32 (outptr, ch);                               \
4412     outptr += 4;                                  \
4413   }
4414 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4415 #define ONEBYTE_BODY \
4416   {                                       \
4417     if (c < 0x80)                                 \
4418       {                                       \
4419     if (c == 0x5c)                                \
4420       return 0xa5;                                \
4421     if (c == 0x7e)                                \
4422       return 0x203e;                              \
4423     return c;                                 \
4424       }                                       \
4425     if (c >= 0xa1 && c <= 0xdf)                           \
4426       return 0xfec0 + c;                              \
4427     return WEOF;                                  \
4428   }
4429 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4430 
4431 
4432 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
4433 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
4434 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4435 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4436 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
4437 #define BODY \
4438   {                                       \
4439     uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr);                          \
4440     const char *cp;                               \
4441                                           \
4442     if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0])))         \
4443       {                                       \
4444     if (ch >= 0x0391 && ch <= 0x0451)                     \
4445       cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x391];                   \
4446     else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa0)                    \
4447       cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x02010];                   \
4448     else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1)               \
4449          && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffef, 1))               \
4450       cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff00];                      \
4451     else                                      \
4452       {                                   \
4453         UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4);                      \
4454         /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4455         cp = "";                                  \
4456       }                                   \
4457       }                                       \
4458     else                                      \
4459       cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch];                            \
4460                                           \
4461     if (__builtin_expect (cp[0] == '\0', 0) && ch != 0)               \
4462       {                                       \
4463     /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4464     STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
4465       }                                       \
4466     else                                      \
4467       {                                       \
4468     *outptr = cp[0];                              \
4469     /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible.  */\
4470     if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
4471       {                                   \
4472         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend))              \
4473           {                                   \
4474         /* The result does not fit into the buffer.  */           \
4475         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4476         break;                                \
4477           }                                   \
4478         *++outptr = cp[1];                            \
4479       }                                   \
4480     ++outptr;                                 \
4481       }                                       \
4482                                           \
4483     inptr += 4;                                   \
4484   }
4485 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4486 #include <iconv/loop.c>
